I have begun,\n', 'And now I give my sensual race the rein:\n', 'Fit thy consent to my sharp appetite;\n', 'Lay by all nicety and prolixious blushes,\n', 'That banish what they sue for; redeem thy brother\n', 'By yielding up thy body to my will;\n', 'Or else he must not only die the death,\n', 'But thy unkindness shall his death draw out\n', 'To lingering sufferance. Did I tell this,\n', 'Who would believe me? O perilous mouths,\n', 'That bear in them one and the self-same tongue,\n', 'Either of condemnation or approof;\n', "Bidding the law make court'sy to their will:\n", 'Hooking both right and wrong to the appetite,\n', "To follow as it draws! I'll to my brother:\n", 'Though he hath fallen by prompture of the blood,\n', 'Yet hath he in him such a mind of honour.\n', 'That, had he twenty heads to tender down\n', "On twenty bloody blocks, he'd yield them up,\n", 'Before his sister should her body stoop\n', "To such abhorr'd pollution.\n", 'Then, Isabel, live chaste, and, brother, die:\n', 'More than our brother is our chastity.\n', "I'll tell him yet of Angelo's request,\n", "And fit his mind to death, for his soul's rest.\n"]], ['DUKE_VINCENTIO', ['Be absolute for death; either death or life\n', 'Shall thereby be the sweeter. Reason thus with life:\n', 'If I do lose thee, I do lose a thing\n', 'That none but fools would keep: a breath thou art,\n', "That dost this habitation, where thou keep'st,\n", "Hourly afflict: merely, thou art death's fool;\n", "For him thou labour'st by thy flight to shun\n", "And yet runn'st toward him still. Thou art not noble;\n", "For all the accommodations that thou bear'st\n", "Are nursed by baseness. Thou'rt by no means valiant;\n", 'For thou dost fear the soft and tender fork\n', 'Of a poor worm. Thou hast nor youth nor age,\n', 'Dreaming on both; when thou art old and rich,\n', 'Thou hast neither heat, affection, limb, nor beauty,\n', "To make thy riches pleasant. There she lost a noble and\n', 'renowned brother, in his love toward her ever most kind and natural; with him, the portion and sinew of her fortune, her marriage-dowry; with both, her combinate husband, this well-seeming Angelo.\n']], ['ISABELLA', ['Can this be so? did Angelo so leave her?\n']], ['DUKE_VINCENTIO', ['Left her in her tears, and dried not one of them with his comfort; swallowed his vows whole,\n', 'pretending in her discoveries of dishonour.\n']], ['ISABELLA', ['But how out of this can she avail?\n']], ['DUKE_VINCENTIO', ['It is a rupture that you may easily heal: and the cure of it not only saves your brother, but keeps\n', 'you from dishonour in doing it.\n']], ['ISABELLA', ['Show me how, good father.\n']], ['DUKE_VINCENTIO', ['Go you to Angelo; answer his requiring with a plausible obedience; agree with his demands to the point; only refer yourself to this advantage, first, that your stay with him may not be long; that the time may have all shadow and silence in it; and the place answer to convenience. This being granted in course, we shall advise this wronged maid to stead up your appointment, go in your place; if the encounter acknowledge itself hereafter, it may compel him to her recompense: and here, by this, is your brother saved, your honour untainted, the poor Mariana advantaged, and the corrupt deputy scaled. There she lost a noble and\n', 'renowned brother, in his love toward her ever most kind and natural; with him, the portion and sinew of her fortune, her marriage-dowry; with both, her combinate husband, this well-seeming Angelo.\n']], ['ISABELLA', ['Can this be so? did Angelo so leave her?\n']], ['DUKE_VINCENTIO', ['Left her in her tears, and dried not one of them with his comfort; swallowed his vows whole,\n', 'pretending in her discoveries of dishonour.\n']], ['ISABELLA', ['But how out of this can she avail?\n']], ['DUKE_VINCENTIO', ['It is a rupture that you may easily heal: and the cure of it not only saves your brother, but keeps\n', 'you from dishonour in doing it.\n']], ['ISABELLA', ['Show me how, good father.\n']], ['DUKE_VINCENTIO', ['Go you to Angelo; answer his requiring with a plausible obedience; agree with his demands to the point; only refer yourself to this advantage, first, that your stay with him may not be long; that the time may have all shadow and silence in it; and the place answer to convenience. This being granted in course, we shall advise this wronged maid to stead up your appointment, go in your place; if the encounter acknowledge itself hereafter, it may compel him to her recompense: and here, by this, is your brother saved, your honour untainted, the poor Mariana advantaged, and the corrupt deputy scaled. O perilous mouths,\n', 'That bear in them one and the self-same tongue,\n', 'Either of condemnation or approof;\n', "Bidding the law make court'sy to their will:\n", 'Hooking both right and wrong to the appetite,\n', "To follow as it draws! Thou hast nor youth nor age,\n', 'Dreaming on both; when thou art old and rich,\n', 'Thou hast neither heat, affection, limb, nor beauty,\n', "To make thy riches pleasant.
